id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_body" class="ajax__tab_body ajax__scroll_vert"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><font size="3"><strong><span>SIG SAUER </span></strong></font><p></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><font size="3"><strong><span>P226 MK25, 9mm, Navy SEAL W/DoD Markings, 3 15 Round Magazines</span></strong></font></p> <p><span>Great find: the SIG SAUER P226 MK25-&nbsp;</span><span>identical to the pistol carried by the U.S. Navy SEALs.</span></p> <p><span>The P226 pistol sets the standard by which all other combat handguns are measured. The exceptional ergonomics and balance make this fullsize pistol easy to handle. Its longer barrel yields better ballistic performance and accuracy. The P226 MK25 is identical to the pistol carried by the U.S. Navy SEALs-the fleets special warfare operators.</span></p> <p><font size="2"><span>This railed P226 MK25 is chambered in 9mm and engraved with an anchor on the left side of the slide. Dept of Defense UID marked on right side of slide.</span></font></p> <p>Unique identification, or UID, is the asset tracking method in which the Department of Defense manages its inventory.</p> <p>The DoD UID program requires all tangible item that are warehoused, supplied, issued or made by a branch of the Department of Defense to be uniquely identified. The UID must distinguish the item from all others, so that the item may be tracked and monitored throughout its entire lifetime within the DoD system.</p> <p>UID is often compared to the social security numbering system. Like a social security number, the UID mark is unique to the item and it identifies the item throughout the span of its lifetime without ever being modified.</p> <p><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/sig-sauer/sig_mk25_b.jpg" alt="" width="372" height="323"></p> <p><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/sig-sauer/sig_mk25_c.jpg" alt="" gun to the range I can say that it's a fine pistol and accurate too. Pro's Big bright night sights that are easy to pick up in a dark room Crisp smooth 10# trigger 3 15 round mags included Great grips And incredibly well built Cons Not many. The weight may be too much for some this is a full size semi auto. And the lack of any safety levers may put off those more focused on safety. But all in all a very well built pistol representative of its p226 pedigree.
